<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dal.html>dal</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:dal.html>dal</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dalą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dal.html>dal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dalen.html>dalen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dalletje.html>dalletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>valley</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_5">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dal.html>dal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dal.html>dallen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dalletje.html>dalletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a type of stone to pave the floor with, flagstone</li></ol>

***dalen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dalen.html>dalen</a> (6929)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dālen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dalon</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dal.html>dal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">valley</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>. Derived in Old Dutch times, and apparently only shared with Low Saxon. The regular Germanic word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> now acquired a more specific sense of “stumble” or “drop uncontrolledly”.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dalen.html>dalen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to descend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decrease, to drop</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:damast.html>damast</a> (70515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">damas</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">Damas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:damascus.html>Damascus</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the Syrian city it originates from.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:damast.html>damast</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:damasten.html>damasten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The fabric damask</li>
<li>A similarly decorative, 'floral' pattern, notably made on finely worked metal using biting chemicals</li></ol>

***dampkring.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dampkring.html>dampkring</a> (28818)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">damp</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kring.html>kring</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dampkring.html>dampkring</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dampkringen.html>dampkringen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dampkring.html>dampkringetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>atmosphere of a planet or satellite <span class="defdate">[18th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>2015</b> December 14, Govert <a href = vnd.unilang:schilling.html>Schilling</a>, "'<a href = vnd.unilang:droge.html>Droge</a>' exoplaneten <a href = vnd.unilang:blijken.html>blijken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nat.html>nat</a>", <i>Volkskrant</i>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>Door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:allerlei.html>allerlei</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:golflengte.html>golflengten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:metingen.html>metingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ontdekten.html>ontdekten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wolken.html>wolken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> heiige <a href = vnd.unilang:lagen.html>lagen</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dampkringen.html>dampkringen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sommige.html>sommige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:planeten.html>planeten</a>.
<dl><dd>By performing measurements on all <a href = vnd.unilang:kinds.html>kinds</a> of wavelengths, they also discovered <a href = vnd.unilang:clouds.html>clouds</a> and unclear layers in the <b>atmospheres</b> of some planets.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Unlike <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:atmosfeer.html>atmosfeer</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dampkring.html>dampkring</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> never used as a physical unit for general use. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also not commonly used for stellar atmospheres, nor figuratively for an <a href = vnd.unilang:ambiance.html>ambiance</a>.
</p>

***dan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> (38)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>then, at that time <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in the future</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>Morgen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beter.html>beter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Tomorrow the weather will be better, but then I must go to work again.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>then, after that
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eerst.html>Eerst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tanden.html>tanden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:poetsen.html>poetsen</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">First you need to brush your teeth, then you may go to <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>then, in that case
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geregend.html>geregend</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:gesneeuwd.html>gesneeuwd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veilig.html>veilig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">If it <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> not rained or snowed, then the car must still be safe.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The adverb <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> almost obligatorily used in Dutch after an imperative with a preceding conditional clause:
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>hebt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bezoekt.html>bezoekt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:ieder.html>ieder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geval.html>geval</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haven.html>haven</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">If you have the time, then be sure to visit the harbour.</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in the past</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a></span></li></ul>

***dank.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dank.html>dank</a> (162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">danc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thank</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þankaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>gratitude, <a href = vnd.unilang:thanks.html>thanks</a></li>
<li>show/token of recognition</li>
<li>reward, recompense</li></ol>

***daredevil.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:daredevil.html>daredevil</a> (70501)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dare</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">devil</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:daredevil.html>daredevil</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">daredevils</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person who engages in very risky behavior, especially one who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> motivated by a craving for excitement or attention. <span class="defdate">[from 1794]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:adrenaline.html>adrenaline</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:junkie.html>junkie</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">adventurer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">thrill-seeker</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>Even</a> as a youngster, <a href = vnd.unilang:steven.html>Steven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a bit of a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:daredevil.html>daredevil</a></b> riding up homemade wooden <a href = vnd.unilang:ramp.html>ramps</a> on his BMX.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:daredevil.html>daredevil</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:daredevil.html>daredevil</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:daredevil.html>daredevil</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Recklessly bold; adventurous. <span class="defdate">[from 1832]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The climatic scene of “Rebel without a Cause” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the group of very <b><a href = vnd.unilang:daredevil.html>daredevil</a></b> teens playing chicken.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:daredevil.html>daredevil</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">daredevils</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">daredevilling</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">daredeviling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">daredevilled</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">daredeviled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To behave in a reckless, adventurous, or physically risky manner</li></ol>
</body>

***darmspoeling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:darmspoeling.html>darmspoeling</a> (57778)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:darm.html>darm</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">spoeling</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:darmspoeling.html>darmspoeling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:darmspoelingen.html>darmspoelingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:darmspoeling.html>darmspoelinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">enema</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">clyster</span> <span class="defdate">[from late 17th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1696</b>, Stephanus Blankaart (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Steven_Blankaart" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Steven Blankaart"><a href = vnd.unilang:steven.html>Steven</a> Blankaart</a>), <i>Nieuw-ligtende praktyk <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> medecinen</i>, 5th ed., page 334.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maakt.html>Maakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b>darmſpoeling</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <i>ſpaanse ſeep <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a></i>, of <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:zout.html>zout</a>, oly</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>Bier</a></i>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Prepare a <b>clyster</b> of Spanish soap and <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>, or of salt, oil and <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dertel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">derten</i>; further etymology unclear. ***dat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> (6)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">that</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þat</i>, neuter form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sa</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>das</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">that</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>that (neuter); <span class="use-with-mention">referring to a thing or a person further away.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>that</b> house</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>that</b> child</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><br />
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">demonstrative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> that, that there
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>that</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension<span class="ib-comma">,</span> demonstrative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> clipping of <b><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:datzelfde.html>datzelfde</a></span></b></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> that same (thig), the aforementioned
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">–Voordat <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weggaat.html>weggaat</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zet.html>zet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afval.html>afval</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:buiten.html>buiten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alsjeblieft.html>alsjeblieft</a>!<br />–Okee, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>).</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">–Before you leave, take the rubbish out please!<br />–Okay, I will do <b>that</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> who, which, that
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ken.html>ken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I know a girl <b>who</b> can do that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">exophoric</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> that, those (regardless of gender and number)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>That</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Those</b> are <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This pronoun can combine with a preposition to form a pronominal adverb. When this occurs, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> changed into its adverbial/locative counterpart <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></i>. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.
</p><p>A preceding comma may alter the meaning of a clause starting with a relative pronoun. Compare the following sentences:
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gaf.html>gaf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I returned the book <b>that</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> white. (The white book specifically, not another)</span></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gaf.html>gaf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I returned the book, <b>which</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> white. (The book happened to be white)</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_3">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>that
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I saw <b>that</b> it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> good.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***databank.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:databank.html>databank</a> (16864)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:databank.html>databank</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">data</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bank</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bank, supply</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:databank.html>databank</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:databanken.html>databanken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:databank.html>databankje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
